Source Code

This source code is very close to the Apollo Guidance Computer software for the Apollo 13 Lunar module. This revision of the Luminary 131 program is from December of 1969, whereas there was a later revision in January of 1970, and still another revision in February, which is the code that flew on the mission. As far as this transcription is concerned, it was originally from a copy made in 1991 of a printout from the collection of AGC developer Don Eyles for collector David Craig. It was subsequently scanned by Gary Neff, reprocessed for online presentation at the now-discontinued History of Recent Science and Technology (HRST) website of MIT's Dibner Institute (the full-quality scans being discarded in the process), and finally transcribed by Ron Burkey for the Virtual AGC Project. Although a high-quality replacement scan for a completely illegible page was later provided by Gary Neff, the reduced legibility of the reprocessed HRST posting nevertheless caused many errors to be introduced into the transcription. Accordingly, a second scan of the same physical printout was made in 2017 for the Virtual AGC Project's collection at the Internet Archive, and used to correct the transcription errors. All of the scanned materials mentioned, as well as other Luminary 131 related material, are available online. Don Eyles apprently made additional hand-written notes in printout between 1991 and 2017, so the two scans are not identical in that respect. The page-headings in the printout read, in part:
	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date the printout was made, not the date on which the program revision was released, although these happen to be very close together.

016357,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME_BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016358,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
016359,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
016360,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13.
016361,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
016362,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
016363,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
016364,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
016365,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 392-475
016366,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016367,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo

016391,000037:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016392,000038:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016393,000039:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016394,000040:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016395,000041: 
016396,000042:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016397,000043: 
016398,000044:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016399,000045:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016400,000046:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016401,000047:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016402,000048: 
016403,000049:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016404,000050:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016405,000051:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016406,000052:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016407,000053:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016408,000054: 
016409,000055:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016410,000056:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016411,000057:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016412,000058:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016413,000059: 
016414,000060:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016415,000061:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016416,000062: 
016417,000063:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016418,000064: 
016419,000065:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016420,000066:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016421,000067:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016422,000068:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016423,000069:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016424,000070: 
016425,000071:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016426,000072:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016427,000073:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016428,000074:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016429,000075: 
016430,000076:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016431,000077:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016432,000078:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016433,000079:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016434,000080:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016435,000081: 
016436,000082:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016437,000083: 
016438,000084:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016439,000085:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016440,000086:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 393 

016442,000088:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016443,000089:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016444,000090:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016445,000091:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016446,000092:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016447,000093:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016448,000094:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016449,000095:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016450,000096:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016451,000097:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016452,000098: 
016453,000099:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016454,000100:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016455,000101:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016456,000102: 
016457,000103:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016458,000104: 
016459,000105:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016460,000106:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016461,000107:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016462,000108: 
016463,000109:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016464,000110:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016465,000111:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016466,000112:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016467,000113:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016468,000114:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016469,000115:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016470,000116: 
016471,000117:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016472,000118:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016473,000119: 
016474,000120:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016475,000121: 
016476,000122:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016477,000123:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016478,000124:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016479,000125:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016480,000126: 
016481,000127:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016482,000128: 
016483,000129:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016484,000130:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016485,000131:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016486,000132:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016487,000133: 
016488,000134:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 394 

016490,000136:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016491,000137: 
016492,000138:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016493,000139: 
016494,000140:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016495,000141:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016496,000142: 
016497,000143:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016498,000144:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016499,000145:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016500,000146:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016501,000147: 
016502,000148:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016503,000149:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016504,000150: 
016505,000151:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016506,000152:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016507,000153:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016508,000154:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016509,000155: 
016510,000156:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016511,000157:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016512,000158: 
016513,000159:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016514,000160:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
016515,000161: 
016516,000162:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016517,000163: 
016518,000164:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016519,000165:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016520,000166:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016521,000167:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016522,000168: 
016523,000169:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016524,000170:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016525,000171: 
016526,000172:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016527,000173:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016528,000174: 
016529,000175:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016530,000176:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016531,000177:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016532,000178: 
016533,000179:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016534,000180: 
016535,000181:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016536,000182:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 395 

016538,000184:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016539,000185:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016540,000186: 
016541,000187:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016542,000188: 
016543,000189: 
016544,000190:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016545,000191: 
016546,000192:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016547,000193:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016548,000194:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
016549,000195:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016550,000196:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016551,000197:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016552,000198:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016553,000199:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016554,000200:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016555,000201:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016556,000202:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016557,000203:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016558,000204:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016559,000205:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016560,000206:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
016561,000207:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016562,000208:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016563,000209:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016564,000210:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016565,000211:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016566,000212:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016567,000213:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016568,000214:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
016569,000215:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016570,000216:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
016571,000217:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016572,000218:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016573,000219:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016574,000220:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016575,000221:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016576,000222:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016577,000223:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016578,000224:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016579,000225:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016580,000226:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016581,000227:

016638,000284:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
016639,000285:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
016640,000286:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
016641,000287:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
016642,000288:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
016643,000289:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
016644,000290:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
016645,000291:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016646,000292:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016647,000293:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016648,000294:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016649,000295:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016650,000296:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
016651,000297:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016652,000298:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
016653,000299:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016654,000300: 
016655,000301:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016656,000302: 
016657,000303:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016658,000304: 
016659,000305:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016660,000306:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016661,000307:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016662,000308:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016663,000309:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016664,000310: 
016665,000311:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016666,000312: 
016667,000313:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016668,000314: 
016669,000315:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016670,000316:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016671,000317:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016672,000318: 
016673,000319:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016674,000320: 
016675,000321:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016676,000322: 
016677,000323:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016678,000324:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
016679,000325:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016680,000326: 
016681,000327:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016682,000328:

Page 398 

016684,000330:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016685,000331:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
016686,000332:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
016687,000333:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
016688,000334:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
016689,000335:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
016690,000336:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
016691,000337:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
016692,000338:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
016693,000339:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
016694,000340:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
016695,000341:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
016696,000342: 
016697,000343:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016698,000344:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016699,000345:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016700,000346:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016701,000347:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016702,000348:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016703,000349: 
016704,000350:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016705,000351:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
016706,000352:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
016707,000353:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
016708,000354:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
016709,000355:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
016710,000356: 
016711,000357:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016712,000358: 
016713,000359:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016714,000360:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
016715,000361:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
016716,000362:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
016717,000363:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
016718,000364:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
016719,000365:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
016720,000366:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
016721,000367:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
016722,000368:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
016723,000369:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
016724,000370: 
016725,000371:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016726,000372: 
016727,000373:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016728,000374:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
016729,000375:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016730,000376:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016731,000377:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016732,000378:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 399 

016734,000380:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016735,000381:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016736,000382:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016737,000383:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016738,000384:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016739,000385:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016740,000386:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016741,000387:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
016742,000388: 
016743,000389:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016744,000390: 
016745,000391:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
016746,000392:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
016747,000393:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
016748,000394:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
016749,000395:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
016750,000396:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
016751,000397:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
016752,000398:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
016753,000399:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
016754,000400:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
016755,000401:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
016756,000402: 
016757,000403:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016758,000404: 
016759,000405:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016760,000406:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016761,000407:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
016762,000408:

017160,000806:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
017161,000807:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
017162,000808:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
017163,000809: 
017164,000810:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
017165,000811:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
017166,000812:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

017451,001097:

Page 415 

017453,001099:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017454,001100: 
017455,001101:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017456,001102:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
017457,001103:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017458,001104:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017459,001105:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017460,001106: 
017461,001107:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017462,001108:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017463,001109: 
017464,001110:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017465,001111: 
017466,001112:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017467,001113:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017468,001114:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017469,001115: 
017470,001116:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017471,001117:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017472,001118:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017473,001119:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017474,001120:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017475,001121:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017476,001122: 
017477,001123:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017478,001124:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017479,001125:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017480,001126:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017481,001127:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017482,001128: 
017483,001129:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017484,001130:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017485,001131: 
017486,001132:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017487,001133: 
017488,001134:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017489,001135:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017490,001136:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017491,001137:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017492,001138:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017493,001139: 
017494,001140:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017495,001141:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017496,001142:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017497,001143: 
017498,001144:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017499,001145:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017500,001146: 
017501,001147:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017502,001148:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
017503,001149:

Page 416 

017505,001151:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017506,001152: 
017507,001153: 41,2355           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
017508,001154: 41,2356           02426                           TC       COMPTEST

018053,001699: 
018054,001700:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
018055,001701:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018056,001702:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018057,001703:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018058,001704:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
018059,001705:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.
018060,001706:

018083,001729:                                                                                                  #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
018084,001730:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY          1) DECIMAL MACHINE

018679,002325: 42,3605           04145                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
018680,002326: 42,3606                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
018681,002327:

Page 441 

018683,002329:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018684,002330:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018685,002331:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018686,002332:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018687,002333:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018688,002334: 
018689,002335:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018690,002336:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018691,002337:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
018692,002338:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
018693,002339:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018694,002340:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018695,002341:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018696,002342: 
018697,002343:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018698,002344:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018699,002345:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018700,002346: 
018701,002347:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,

018833,002479:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018834,002480:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
018835,002481:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018836,002482:                                                                                                  #  
018837,002483:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018838,002484: 
018839,002485:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018840,002486:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018841,002487:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018842,002488: 
018843,002489:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018844,002490:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018845,002491:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018846,002492: 
018847,002493: 41,3400           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018848,002494: 41,3401           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018849,002495: 41,3402           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018850,002496: 41,3403           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018851,002497: 41,3404           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018852,002498: 41,3405           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018853,002499: 41,3406           03410                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018854,002500: 41,3407           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019253,002899:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
019254,002900:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE.  SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,

019262,002908:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
019263,002909:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 454 

019265,002911: 
019266,002912:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019267,002913: 
019268,002914:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019269,002915: 
019270,002916:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019271,002917:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019272,002918:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019273,002919:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019274,002920: 
019275,002921:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019276,002922:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019277,002923:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019278,002924: 
019279,002925:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019280,002926:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019281,002927:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019282,002928:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019283,002929:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019284,002930:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019285,002931:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019286,002932:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019287,002933:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019288,002934:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019289,002935:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019290,002936: 
019291,002937: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019292,002938: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019293,002939: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019294,002940: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019295,002941: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019296,002942: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019297,002943: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019298,002944: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019299,002945: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019300,002946: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019301,002947: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019302,002948: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019303,002949: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019304,002950: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019305,002951: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019306,002952: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019307,002953: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019308,002954: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019309,002955: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019310,002956: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019311,002957: 
019312,002958: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019313,002959:

Page 455 

019315,002961:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
019316,002962:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019317,002963:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019318,002964:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019319,002965:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019320,002966: 
019321,002967:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019322,002968:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
019323,002969:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019324,002970: 
019325,002971:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019326,002972:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019327,002973: 
019328,002974:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019329,002975:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019330,002976:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019331,002977:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019332,002978:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019333,002979: 
019334,002980:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019335,002981:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019336,002982:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019337,002983:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019338,002984: 
019339,002985:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019340,002986:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019341,002987:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019342,002988:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019343,002989:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019344,002990:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019345,002991:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019346,002992: 
019347,002993:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019348,002994:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019349,002995: 
019350,002996:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019351,002997:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019352,002998: 
019353,002999:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019354,003000:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019355,003001: 
019356,003002:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019357,003003:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019358,003004:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019359,003005:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019360,003006:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019361,003007:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019362,003008:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019363,003009: 
019364,003010:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 456 

019366,003012:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019367,003013:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019368,003014:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019369,003015:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019370,003016:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
019371,003017:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019372,003018:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019373,003019:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019374,003020:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019375,003021: 
019376,003022:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019377,003023:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019378,003024: 
019379,003025:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019380,003026: 
019381,003027:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

019410,003056:    4203           05165                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
019411,003057:
