019489,003135:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019490,003136:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019491,003137:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019492,003138:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019493,003139:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019494,003140:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019495,003141: 
019496,003142:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
019497,003143:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019498,003144:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019499,003145:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019500,003146:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
019501,003147: 
019502,003148:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019503,003149:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019504,003150:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019505,003151:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019506,003152:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019507,003153:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019508,003154:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019509,003155:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019510,003156:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019511,003157:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019512,003158: 
019513,003159:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 459 

019515,003161:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019516,003162:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019517,003163:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019518,003164:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019519,003165:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
019520,003166: 
019521,003167:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019522,003168:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019523,003169:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019524,003170:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019525,003171:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019526,003172:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019527,003173:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019528,003174:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019529,003175: 
019530,003176:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019531,003177: 
019532,003178:    4220           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.

019574,003220:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019575,003221:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.

019856,003502:

Page 467 

019858,003504:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019859,003505: 
019860,003506:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019861,003507:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019862,003508:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019863,003509:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019864,003510: 
019865,003511:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019866,003512:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
019867,003513:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
019868,003514:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019869,003515:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019870,003516:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019871,003517:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019872,003518: 
019873,003519:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019874,003520:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019875,003521:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019876,003522:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019877,003523:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019878,003524: 
019879,003525:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019880,003526:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019881,003527:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019882,003528:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019883,003529:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019884,003530: 
019885,003531:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019886,003532:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019887,003533:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019888,003534: 
019889,003535: 
019890,003536:                                                                                                  #  .
019891,003537: 
019892,003538: 
019893,003539:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019894,003540:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019895,003541:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019896,003542:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019897,003543: 
019898,003544:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019899,003545:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019900,003546:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019901,003547: 
019902,003548:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019903,003549:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
019904,003550:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 468 

019906,003552:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019907,003553: 
019908,003554:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019909,003555:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019910,003556:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019911,003557:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019912,003558:    4443           10633                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019913,003559:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019914,003560: 
019915,003561:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019916,003562:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019917,003563: 
019918,003564: 04,2633                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019919,003565: 04,2633                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019920,003566: 04,2633           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019921,003567: 04,2634           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019922,003568: 04,2635           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019923,003569: 04,2636           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019924,003570: 04,2637           30001                           CA       L                                     
019925,003571: 04,2640           55042                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019926,003572: 04,2641           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019927,003573: 
019928,003574:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019929,003575:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019930,003576:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019931,003577:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019932,003578:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019933,003579: 
019934,003580:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019935,003581:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019936,003582:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019937,003583:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019938,003584:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019939,003585:    4450           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019940,003586:    4451           61011                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019941,003587:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019942,003588:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019943,003589:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019944,003590:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019945,003591:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019946,003592:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019947,003593: 
019948,003594:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019949,003595:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019950,003596:

020102,003748:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020103,003749:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020104,003750:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020105,003751: 
020106,003752:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020107,003753:                                                                                                  #  
020108,003754:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020109,003755:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
